-----title
杭州
-----detail

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年1月</a>　春正月，从驾至临安，有渡钱塘诗。作品：《渡江》<div id='poem_153104' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153104' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_153104'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153104'>江南非不好，楚客自生哀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153104'>摇楫天平渡，迎人树欲来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153104'>雨馀吴岫立，日照海门开。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153104'>虽异中原险，方隅亦壮哉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153104'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_153104_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　是春，在临安。作品：《夙兴》《幽窗》<div id='poem_153214' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153214' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_153214'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153214'>美哉木枕与菅席，无耐<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作禁）</span>当兴戴朝帻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153214'>巷南巷北闻锻声，舍后舍前唯月色。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153214'>事国无功端未去，竹舆伊鸦犹昨日。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153214'>不见武林城里事，繁华梦觉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>生荆棘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153214'>成坏<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作败）</span>由来几古今，乾坤但可著山泽。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1118')">1118年</a>　简斋在京师。是秋多雨。作品：《夜雨》《连雨不能出有怀同年陈国佐》<div id='poem_153040' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153040' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153040'>蝉声未足秋风起，木叶俱鸣夜雨来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153040'>棋局可观浮世理，灯花应为好诗开。<div 原注：王俊乂字尧明，海陵人。宣和元年赐上舍第，与承事郎两学职事。四年，任太学博士。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153224'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153224'>奏书初不待<span class='link' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_152877' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/152877?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_152877_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_152877'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_152877'>忆看梅雪缟中庭，转眼桃梢无数青。<div id='poem_sentence_0_152877_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_152877'>万事一身双鬓发，竹床攲卧<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作枕）</span>数窗棂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_152877_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_152877'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_152877_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　为太学博士，与同官綦崇礼力救文弊，黜三舍偶丽体，去王氏之论，而尊用程氏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　为诸生陈道醇之兄作《颐轩记》<div id='poem_1236332' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236332' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236332?labeling=true' target='_blank'>颐轩记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_1236332")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236332_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236332'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236332'>余客汝州，识治狱掾陈德润，与之语，肺肝无溪壑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236332_comment'></div>奔走百僚之底，未尝一日有怠容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236332_comment'></div>后官太学，而其弟道醇肄业焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236332_comment'></div>宦学万里，贫不振，天子幸学，官之，澹然不色喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236332_comment'></div>余以是愧其兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236332_comment'></div>道醇间语曰：「我又有隐居不仕之兄，庐西山之下，其燕居所榜之曰『颐轩』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236332_comment'></div>前崖岫之崷崒，后涧壑之琮琤，烟云草木，晦明寒暑，出天地之奇变，以娱轩中之人，世之得丧利害，无所经其怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236332_comment'></div>我与汝州掾，心不能忘也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236332_comment'></div>余面赞之曰：「钟皓有兄不仕，皓亦逡巡难进，居官有闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236332_comment'></div>何点栖遁求志，而其子弟遗进退之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236332_comment'></div>后世莫訾焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236332_comment'></div>而今而后，知二子之师友不在他，在颐轩尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236332_comment'></div>于其归也，申以告之曰：「大丈夫用世非难也，无愧于颐轩之兄为难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236332_comment'></div>其亦告于颐轩之兄，不仕非难也，行义风烈有闻于乡里，无愧乎前之山、后之涧为难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236332_comment'></div>古之君子，居也，其仕也，其道一也而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236332_comment'></div>二子方将为轩冕所縻，异日风绩振耀，而用舍行藏可观可纪，则颐轩之进德亦可占矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236332_comment'></div>道醇曰：「是盖颐轩之记，盍书之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236332_comment'></div>乃录大略，使归书之其壁，且以告德润云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236332_comment'></div>洛阳陈去非记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1236332_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年7月</a>　徽宗见所赋《墨梅》诗，善之，亟命召对，有见晚之叹，除秘书省著作佐郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年7月</a>　在京师。与张元干、吕本中等游慧林寺，分韵赋诗。作品：《游慧林寺以三峡炎蒸定有无为韵得定字是日欲逃暑阁下而守阁童子持不可》<div id='poem_153356' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153356' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/153356?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游慧林寺以三峡<span class='inlineComment2'>（须溪本作伏）</span>炎蒸定有无为韵得定字是日欲逃暑阁下而守阁童子持不可</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_153356")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_153356_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153356'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153356'>我如东郊马，攲<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>侧甘瘦病。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153356'>今晨举足轻，起行得幽胜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153356'>抚窗唤懒融，槁面初出定。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153356'>眼中<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>无长物，坐久炉烟正。<div id='poem_content_153244'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153244'>闭<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>门睡过春，出门绿满城。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153244'>八关池上柳，絮罢但藏莺。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153244'>世故剧千猬，今朝此闲行。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153244'>草木随时好，客恨终难平。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153244'>寺有石壁胜，诗无康乐声。<div id='poem_sentence_4_153244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_153244'>扶鞍不得上，新月水中生。<div id='poem_sentence_5_153244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_153244'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_153244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_153244'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_153244_0'>⑴ 原作闲，据须溪本、四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_153244_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年</a>　居陈留。作品：《题酒务壁》<div id='poem_153387' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153387' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_153387'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153387'>野马本不羁，无奈卯与申。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153387'>当时彭泽令，定是英雄人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153387'>客来两绳床，客去一欠伸。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153387'>市声自杂沓，炉烟自轮囷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153387'>莺声时节改，杏叶雨气新。<div id='poem_sentence_4_153387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_153387'>佳句忽堕前，追摹已难真。<div id='poem_sentence_5_153387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_153387'>自题西轩壁，不杂徐庾尘<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《增广笺注简斋诗集》卷一三）</span>。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年</a>　居陈留，秋夜咏月。作品：《秋夜咏月》<div id='poem_153287' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153287' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_153287'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153287'>庭树日日疏，稍觉夜月添。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153287'>推愁了此段，卷我三间帘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153287'>黄花墙阴远，白发露气严。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153287'>平生六尺影，随我送凉炎。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153287'>踏破千忧地，投老乃自嫌。<div id='poem_sentence_4_153287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_153287'>尚想采石江，宫锦映霜蟾。<div id='poem_sentence_5_153287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_153287'>夜半赋诗成，起舞鱼龙兼。<div id='poem_sentence_6_153287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_153287'>办此讵难事，取快端宜廉。<div id='poem_sentence_7_153287_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_153287'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_153287_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年</a>　居陈留。是冬，咏诸诗。作品：《入城》《夜步堤上三首》《早起》《晚步》<div id='poem_153260' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153260' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/153260?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夜步堤上三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_153260_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153260'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153260'>世故生白发，意行无与期。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153260'>平生木上座，临老始相知。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153260'>月中沙岸永，岁暮河流迟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153260'>留侯庙前柳，叶尽空离离。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153260'>百年信难料，剩赋奇绝诗。<div id='poem_sentence_4_153260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_153260'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_153260_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_153259' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153259' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/153259?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_153259_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153259'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153259'>人间<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_153259", 153259, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>睡声</span>起，幽子方独步<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作立）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153259'>倚杖看白云，亭亭水中度。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153259'>十月雁背高，三更河流去。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153259'>物生各扰扰，念此煎百虑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153259'>聊将忧世心，数遍桥西树。<div id='poem_sentence_4_153259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_153259'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_153259_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_153258' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153258' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/153258?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_153258_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153258'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153258'>旋买青芒鞋，去踏沙头月。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153258_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153258'>争教冠盖地，著此影突兀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153258_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153258'>树寒栖鸟动，风转孤管发。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153258_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153258'>月色夜夜佳，人生事如发。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153258_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153258'>梦中续清游，浓露湿银阙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_153258_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_153258'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_153258_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年</a>　居陈留，尝同杨运干、黄秀才村西买山药，又观取鱼于窦家池，作诗赋。作品：《玉延赋》《放鱼赋》《同杨运干黄秀才村西买山药》《同二子观取鱼于窦家池以钱得数斗置驿西野塘中圉圉而逝我辈皆欣然也》<div id='poem_1236309' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236309' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236309?labeling=true' target='_blank'>玉延赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_1236309")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236309_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236309'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236309'>吾闻阳公之田，不垦不耕，爰播盈斗，可获连城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236309_comment'></div>资阴阳之淑气，孕天地之至精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236309_comment'></div>蜿蜒赤埴之腴，煌扈白虹之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236309_comment'></div>惊山水之润发，冒朝采之馀荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236309_comment'></div>逮百嘉之泽尽，候此玉之丰成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236309_comment'></div>王公大人方以不贪为宝，辞秦玉而陋楚珩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236309_comment'></div>虽三献其奚售，乃举贽于老生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236309_comment'></div>老生囊中之法未试，腹内之雷久鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236309_comment'></div>搴石鼎而自濯，据豕腹之彭亨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236309_comment'></div>春江浩其波涛，远壑飒以松声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236309_comment'></div>俄白云之涨谷，乱双眼于晦明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236309_comment'></div>擅人间之三绝，色味胜而香清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236309_comment'></div>捧杯盂而笑领，映牖户之新晴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236309_comment'></div>斥去懒残之芋，尽弃接舆之菁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236309_comment'></div>收奇勋于景刻，匕未落而体轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236309_comment'></div>淩厉八仙，扫除三彭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236309_comment'></div>见蓬莱之夷路，接阊阖于初程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236309_comment'></div>彼徇华之大夫，含三生之宿醒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236309_comment'></div>污之以蜂蜜，辱之以羊羹，合尝逸少之炙，同传孝仪之鲭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236309_comment'></div>叹超然之至味，乃陆沈于聋盲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236309_comment'></div>岂皆能于我遇，亦或卿而或烹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236309_comment'></div>起投笔而三叫，驱蛇蚓以纵横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236309_comment'></div>吾何与大夫之迷疾，盖以慰此玉之不平也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1236309_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1236310' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236310' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236310?labeling=true' target='_blank'>放鱼赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_1236310")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236310_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236310'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236310'>仲冬良日，二客过予，请观鱼于窦氏之陂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236310_comment'></div>摄哀而兴，从客往嬉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236310_comment'></div>日澹寒郊，木影陆离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236310_comment'></div>顾道旁之恂异于他日，浩如潮之方滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236310_comment'></div>客曰：「是殆水师不仁，将平地以尽鱼，空其池而寓之斯也，至则水不肤寸矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236310_comment'></div>而百万之鳞，瀺灂声沸，金横玉偃，失据狼狈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236310_comment'></div>赤手下捕，易若拾块，翻倒窟穴，不遗细碎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236310_comment'></div>问其所以得取，则输金钱以买诸窦氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236310_comment'></div>噫嘻！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236310_comment'></div>见鱼之爱其生，与我无异也，奈何使充牣之性命，带噞喁而就脔割，才以易一朝之费？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236310_comment'></div>彼任公子，虽永负于一鱼，而浙河以东，苍梧以北，皆歌舞其赐，则乘除而逆计之，其得失有以相济也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236310_comment'></div>聊解我衣，救尔戢戢，爰得数斗，护以微湿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236310_comment'></div>岂不指动，易生相急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236310_comment'></div>将逸尔于隋沟，资淮海以供给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236310_comment'></div>已趣汤而幸见赦，同伏锧而偶不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236310_comment'></div>其亦知遇我之不可常，而教鲂鱮以慎出入也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1236310_comment'></div>僮奴笑曰：「美则美矣，抑此赐不终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1236310_comment'></div>夫巢梁之禽，智困深丛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1236310_comment'></div>草秀岩下，出山不丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1236310_comment'></div>是鱼安乐于止水之渊久矣，而一旦投之冲沙走石之流，亦鳞败鳍折，未十里而取穷耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1236310_comment'></div>不虞生异，使我辞索，遂用其言，脱鱼再厄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1236310_comment'></div>步驿门而左转，得渺然之平泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1236310_comment'></div>其深黛黑，其浅鉴白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1236310_comment'></div>穷源委而四顾，知我辈之责塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1236310_comment'></div>罄一泻而莫留，乱藻荇之寒碧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1236310_comment'></div>乍圉圉以洋洋，忽四散而莫迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1236310_comment'></div>异乾鱼之还乡，类群鳄之徙宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1236310_comment'></div>念宇宙之伟事，或偶成于戏剧，岂特为今日之一快，吾将候风雷于他夕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1236310_comment'></div>众客欣然，三绕而退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1236310_comment'></div>归泚我笔，以记斯会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1236310_comment'></div>庶几窦氏子闻之，为来岁之戒。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1236310_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_153208' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153208' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/153208?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同杨运干黄秀才村西买山药</a><span class='authorDate'>（1125年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_153208")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_153208_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153208'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153208'>潦缩<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_153208", 153208, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>田路</span>宽，委蛇散腰脚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153208'>胜日三枝杖，村西买山药。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153208'>岗峦相吞去<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作吐）</span>，远木互前却。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153208'>天阴野水明，岁暮竹篱薄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153208'>田翁领客意，发筐堆磊落。<div id='poem_sentence_4_153208_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_153208'>玉质缃色裘，用世乃见缚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153206'>闭户<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>读书生白发，闲向村东看鱼穴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153206_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153071'>以我千金帚，逢君万斛船。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153071'>要知穷有自，未觉懒相先。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153071'>盆盎三年梦，篇章四海传。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153071'>匆匆秣归马，离恨满霜天。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153071'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_153071_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_152996' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_152996' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/152996?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵周教授秋怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_152996")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_152996_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_152996'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_152996'>一官不办作生涯，几见秋风捲岸沙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_152996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_152996'>宋玉有文悲落木，陶潜无酒对黄花。<div id='poem_sentence_1_152996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_152996'>天机衮衮山新瘦，世事悠悠日自斜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_152996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_152996'>误矣载书三十乘，东门何地不宜瓜<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《增广笺注简斋诗集》卷一）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_152996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_152996'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_152996_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
汝州
-----detail

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　简斋丁母忧居汝州，为知州葛胜仲所知，因与陈恬、富直柔诸人相识，而交游日广。作品：《闻葛工部写<华严经>成，随喜赋诗》<div id='poem_153299' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153299' id='poem_sentence_1_153299_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153299'>老郎居尘念不起，法中龙象人师子。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153299_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153299'>前身智永心了然，结习未空犹寄此。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153299_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153299'>怪公聚笔如须弥，经成笔尽手不知。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153034'>梦寐连萧瑟<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作索）</span>，更筹乱晦冥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153034'>云移过吴越，应为洗馀腥<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《增广笺注简斋诗集》卷七）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153034'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_153034_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1121&endYear=1121')">1121年</a>　陈恬赋王秀才藏梁织佛图诗，邀同赋，次韵和之。作品：《陈叔易赋王秀才所藏梁织佛图诗邀同赋因次其韵》<div id='poem_153253' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153253' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_0_153253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153253'>稽首世尊真实相，不比图画填青红。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153253'>意匠经营与佛会，七宝欲动声珑珑。<div id='poem_sentence_4_153253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_153253'>眉间毫光放未尽，指下已带旃檀风。<div id='poem_sentence_5_153253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_153253'>飞梭本是龙变化，挟大威德行神通。<div id='poem_sentence_9_153253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_153253'>那知金臂是正倒，但觉已挫千魔锋。<div id='poem_sentence_10_153253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_153227_1'>② 原注：季申名直柔，郑公曾孙。绍兴初任同知枢密院事。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153227'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153227'>东风知君将出游，玉人迥立林之幽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153227_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153227'>攲墙数苞乃尔瘦，中有万斛江南愁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153227_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153227'>君哦新诗我听莹，句里无尘春色静。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153227_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153227'>人人索笑那得禁，独为君诗起君病。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153227_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153227'>欲语未语令人嗟，桃李回看眼中沙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_153227_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_153227'>同心不见昭仪种，五出时惊公主花。<div id='poem_sentence_5_153227_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_153321_1'>② 原注：东之名元明，通直益之子，文僖公惟演之四世孙也。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153321'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153321'>君不见铜雀台边多事土，走上觚棱荫歌舞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153321_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153321'>馀香分尽垢不除，却寄书林污<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_2_153321'>岂如此瓦凝青膏，冷面不识奸雄曹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153321_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153321'>吕公<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>已去泫馀泣，通谱未许弘农陶。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153321_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153321'>暮年得君真耐久，摩挲玉质云生手。<div id='poem_sentence_6_153321'>西家扑满本弟昆，趣尚清浊何年分。<div id='poem_sentence_6_153321_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_153321'>一朝堕地真瓦砾，莫望韩公无瘗文。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　简斋丁母忧居汝州，与天宁寺僧觉心数相唱和。作品：《和天宁老觉心》《画山水赋》<div id='poem_1236308' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1236308' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1236308?labeling=true' target='_blank'>觉心画山水赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_1236308")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1236308_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1236308'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1236308'>天宁堂中，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1236308", 1236308, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>黄面老禅</span>，四海无人，碧眼视天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1236308_comment'></div>有一居士，山泽之仙，结三生之习气，口不停乎说山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1236308_comment'></div>聊寄答于一笑，夜乃梦乎其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1236308_comment'></div>重岩复岭，亏蔽吐吞，纷应接其未了，万云忽兮归屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1236308_comment'></div>乱晦明于俄顷，存十二之峰峦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1236308_comment'></div>有木偃蹇，樵斤所难，饱千霜与百霆，根不动而意安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1236308_comment'></div>澹山椒之落日，送万古以无言，彼栖乌其何知，方相急而破烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1236308_comment'></div>须臾变灭，所见惟壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1236308_comment'></div>有木上座，梦中侍侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1236308_comment'></div>问上座以何见，口不能于啧啧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1236308_comment'></div>岂彼口之真无，悟前境之非实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1236308_comment'></div>管城子在旁，代对以臆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1236308_comment'></div>忽风雨之骤过，恍向来之所历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1236308_comment'></div>此其画耶，则草木禽鸟，皆似相识；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1236308_comment'></div>抑犹梦耶，则已见囿于笔墨之迹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1236308_comment'></div>居士再至，问以此故，复寄答于一笑，持画疾去。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1236308_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_2_153322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153322'>平生酪奴谤，脉脉气未申。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153322_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153270'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153270'>儿时学道逃悲欢，只今未免忧饥寒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153270'>竹林步兵亦忍辱，长安闭门<span class='inlineComment2'>（须溪本作户）</span>出无仆。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153270'>门前故人拥庐儿，政坐向来甘碌碌。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153270'>公<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作君）</span>不见古人有待良不多，利名溺人甚风波。<div id='poem_sentence_4_153270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_153270'>两翁观光今几时<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，赋归有约时已稽。<div id='poem_sentence_8_153270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_153270'>未暇藏身北山北，且须觅地西枝西。<div id='poem_sentence_9_153270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_153270'>愿从我翁归洗耳，不用妓女污山水。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153328'>云霞映道路，中有迎翠诗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153328'>遥知五斗粟，未办买山资。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153328'>政要百尺楼，了此浮天眉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_153328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_153328'>君方领此意，簿书何急为。<div id='poem_sentence_6_153328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_153328'>众手剧云雨，唯山不瑕疵。<div id='poem_sentence_7_153328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_153328'>当年四老翁，视世轻于芝。<div id='poem_sentence_8_153328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_153328'>坐令山偃蹇，不受人招麾。<div id='poem_sentence_9_153328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_153328'>谁欤楼中客，俯仰与山期。<div id='poem_sentence_10_153328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_153328'>顾要君折腰，督邮真小儿。<div id='poem_sentence_11_153328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_153328'>因之感我意，故岩归已迟。<div id='poem_sentence_12_153328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_153328'>便携灵运屐，不待德璋移。<div id='poem_sentence_13_153328_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_153328'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_153328_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　简斋丁母忧居汝州，是春，陈恬母丧。作品：《陈叔易学士母阮氏挽词二首》<div id='poem_153036' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153036' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/153036?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈叔易学士母阮氏挽词<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_153036")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_153036_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153036'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153036'>典刑奕奕照来今，鹤发鱼轩汝水浔。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153036'>避地梁鸿不偕老，弄乌莱子若为心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153036'>送葬<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>忽见三千乘，奉裞那闻五百金。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153036'>妇德母仪俱不愧，碑铭知已托张林<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：晁说之许铭墓。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153036'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_153036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_153036'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_153036_0'>⑴ 须溪本、四库本作丧</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_153036_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_153035' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153035' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/153035?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_153035_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153035'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153035'>去年披雾识儒先，欲拜萱堂未敢前。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153035'>卢壶要传纱缦业，王裒忽废蓼莪篇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153035'>秀眉隔梦黄垆里，落日驱风丹旐边。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153035'>佛子归真定何处，空令苦泪涨黄泉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153035'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_153035_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　简斋丁母忧居汝州，春末归洛。作品：《留别葛汝州》<div id='poem_153317' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153317' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/153317?labeling=true' target='_blank'>留别葛汝州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>明向公许。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153317'>一时盛德人中骥，四海知名地上虎。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153317'>东序阶墀再靴板，西州杖屦三寒暑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_153317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_153317'>行看入侍玉皇案，与进不待金刚杵。<div id='poem_sentence_8_153317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_153317'>劝公慎勿<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>学孔光，荐士何妨似张禹。<div id='poem_sentence_9_153317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_153317'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_153317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_153317'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_153317_0'>⑴ 原作遍，据四库本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_153317_0'>⑵ 原作物，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_153317_comment'></div></div><br /></div>

商水
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6ae16ae1e24148a4a611d210af8eb785_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6ae16ae1e24148a4a611d210af8eb785");'><span id='6ae16ae1e24148a4a611d210af8eb785_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>，37岁</div><div id='6ae16ae1e24148a4a611d210af8eb785' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年1月</a>　正月，金人犯京师。简斋丁忧，去陈留，出商水。作品：《发商水道中》<div id='poem_152971' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_152971' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/152971?labeling=true' target='_blank'>发商水道中</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_152971")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_152971_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_152971'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_152971'>商水西门语，东风动柳枝。<div id='poem_sentence_0_152971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_152971'>年华入危涕，世事本前期。<div id='poem_sentence_1_152971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_152971'>草草<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_152971", 152971, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>檀公策</span>，茫茫杜老诗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_152971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_152971'>山川马前阔，不敢计归时。<div id='poem_sentence_3_152971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_152971'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_152971_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

舞阳

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　简斋丁忧，去陈留，道舞阳。作品：《次舞阳》<div id='poem_153231' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153231' class='poemTitle id='poem_content_153231'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153231'>客子寒亦行，正月固多阴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
南阳

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　始以简斋自号，作《题简斋》诗。<div id='poem_153390' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153390' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_153390")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_153390_comment'></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153390'>我窗三尺馀，可以阅晦明。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153390'>北省虽巨丽，无此风竹声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153390'>不著散花女，而况使鬼兄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153390'>世间多歧路，居士绳床平。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153390'>未知阮遥集，几屐了平生。<div id='poem_sentence_4_153390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_153390'>领军一屋鞋，千载笑绝缨。<div id='poem_sentence_5_153390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_153390'>槐阴自入户，知我喜新晴。<div id='poem_sentence_6_153390_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_153390'>觅句方未了，简斋真虚名。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　简斋丁忧，去陈留，次南阳，留焉。为邓州天宁寺僧印老作钝庵诗。作品：《印老索钝庵诗》<div id='poem_153188' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153188' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/153188?labeling=true' target='_blank'>印老索钝庵诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_153188")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_153188_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153188'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153188'>人言融公懒，床上揖宾客。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153188_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153188'>我来两忘揖，团团一庵白。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153188_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153188'>戏谈邓州禅，分食天宁麦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153188_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153188'>竹风亦喜我，萧瑟至日夕。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153188_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153188'>出家丈夫事，轩裳<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作冕）</span>本儿剧。<div id='poem_sentence_4_153188_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_153188'>愿香惊馀烟，世故感陈迹。<div id='poem_sentence_5_153188_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_153188'>固应师未钝，使我不安席。<div -----title
房县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2c7cd8e9901041c0a1715a9d966f8cae_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2c7cd8e9901041c0a1715a9d966f8cae");'><span id='2c7cd8e9901041c0a1715a9d966f8cae_link' id='poem_title_153191' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/153191?labeling=true' target='_blank'>正月十二日自房州城遇虏<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>至奔入南山十五日抵回谷张家</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年1月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_153191")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_153191_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_153191_0'>① 虏字，须溪本作金虏</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153191'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153191'>久谓事当尔，岂意身及之。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153191_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153191'>避虏连三年，行半天四维。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153191_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153191'>我非洛豪士，不畏穷谷饥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153191_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153191'>但恨平生意，轻了少陵诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153191_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153191'>今年奔房州，铁马背后驰。<div id='poem_sentence_4_153191_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_153191'>造物亦恶剧，脱命真毫釐。<div id='poem_sentence_5_153191_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_153191'>南山四程云，布袜傲险巇。<div id='poem_sentence_6_153191_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_153191'>篱间老炙背，无意管安危。<div id='poem_sentence_7_153191_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_153191'>知我是朝士，亦复颦其眉。<div id='poem_sentence_8_153191_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_153191'>呼酒软客脚，菜本濯玉肌。<div id='poem_sentence_9_153191_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_153191'>穷途士易德，欢喜不复辞。<div id='poem_sentence_10_153191_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_153191'>向来贪读书，闭户生白髭。<div id='poem_sentence_11_153191_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_153191'>岂知九州内，有山如此奇。<div id='poem_sentence_12_153191_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href='/Writing/153193?labeling=true' target='_blank'>正月十六日夜二绝<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年1月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_153193")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_153193_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153193'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153193'>正月十六夜，竹篱田父家。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153193_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153193'>明月照树影，满山如龙蛇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153193_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_content_152988'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_152988'>胡儿又看绕淮春，叹息犹为国有人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_152988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_152988'>可使翠华周宇县，谁持白羽静风尘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_152988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_152988'>五年天地无穷事，万里江湖见在身。<div id='poem_sentence_2_152988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_152988'>共说金陵<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_152988", 152988, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>龙虎气</span>，放臣迷路感<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_152988", 152988, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>烟津</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_152988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_152988'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_152988_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

岳阳

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　简斋居岳州，闻王鉌附张恭甫舟过湖南，作诗送之。作品：《王应仲欲附张恭甫舟过湖南久不决今日忽闻遂登舟作诗送之并简恭甫》<div id='poem_153179' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153179' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/153179?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王应仲欲附张恭甫舟过湖南久不决今日忽闻遂登舟作诗送之并简恭甫<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_153179")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_153179_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_153179_0'>① id='poem_sentence_2_153179'>从来有名士，不用<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_153179", 153179, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>无名钱</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153179'>披君三径草，分我一味禅。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153179'>胡为黄鹄举，忽上湖南船。<div id='poem_sentence_4_153179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_153179'>竟随文若去，聊伴元礼仙。<div id='poem_sentence_8_153179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_153179'>作诗相棹讴，寄恨馀酸然<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_153241")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_153241_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153241'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153241'>我梦君山好，万里来南州。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153241'>青眉横玉镜，色照城中楼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153241'>胜日空倚眺，经年未成游。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153241'>今朝过山下，贼急不敢留。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153241'>嵌空浪吞吐，荟蔚风飕飗<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作飕，据须溪本改）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_153241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_153241'>龙吟杂虎啸，九夏含三秋。<div id='poem_sentence_5_153241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_153241'>了与遥赏异，况乃行岩幽。<div id='poem_sentence_6_153241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_153241'>蚍蜉何当扫，延伫回我舟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_153241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_153241'>掷去九节筇，褰裳走林丘。<div id='poem_sentence_8_153241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_153241'>会逢湘君降，翠气衣上浮。<div id='poem_sentence_9_153241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_153241'>山椒望苍梧，寄恨舒冥搜。<div id='poem_sentence_10_153241_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_153241'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_153241_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='8977a48b7ae04a29a7d8b2195dc14bfc_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年7月16日</a>　从华容道乌纱还郡，出小江口宿焉，有诗。作品：《自五月二日避寇转徙湖中复从华容道乌纱还郡七月十六日夜半出小江口泊焉徙倚柂楼书十二句》<div id='poem_153132' class='_poem'><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年8月15日</a>　中秋，与任才仲醉于岳阳楼上。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年8月12日</a>　闰八月十二日，过孙伟赏木犀，有诗报王使君接。作品：《闰八月十二日过奇父共坐翠窦轩赏木犀花玲珑满枝光气动人念风日不贷此花无五日香矣而王使君未之知作小诗报之》《再赋二首呈奇父》<div id='poem_152847' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_152847' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/152847?labeling=true' target='_blank'>闰八月十二日过奇父共坐翠窦轩赏木犀花玲珑满枝光气动人念风日不贷此花无五日香矣而王使君未之知作小诗报之<sup class='reference id='poem_sentence_0_152847_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_152847'>极知有日交铜虎，可使无情向木犀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_152847_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_152813'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_152813_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年8月13日</a>　闰八月十三日，郡中修水战之具，大阅燕公楼下，再赋二首，呈王使君。作品：《十三日再赋二首其一以赞使君是日对花赋此韵诗笔落纵横而郡中修水战之具方大阅於燕公楼下也其一自叙所感忆年十五在杭州始识此花皆三丈高木尝赋诗焉》<div id='poem_152774' id='poem_sentence_1_152774_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_152774'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_152774_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　重九前后，与孙、王数相唱酬。作品：《九月八日登高作重九奇父赋三十韵与义拾余意亦赋十二韵》《粹翁用奇父韵赋九日与义同赋兼呈奇父》<div id='poem_153377' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153377' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/153377?labeling=true' target='_blank'>粹翁用奇父韵赋九日与义同赋兼呈奇父</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_sentence_0_153377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153377'>先生守苜蓿，朝士誇茱萸。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153377'>前年邓州城，风雨倾客居。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153377'>何尝疏曲生，曲生自我疏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153377'>岂无登高地，送目与云俱。<div id='poem_sentence_4_153377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_153377'>门生及儿子，劝我升篮舆。<div id='poem_sentence_5_153377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_153377'>出门复入门，戈旆填街衢。<div id='poem_sentence_8_153377'>莫招大夫魂，谁揽使君须。<div id='poem_sentence_8_153377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_153377'>独题怀古句，<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_10_153377'>亦复跻荒戍，日暮野踟蹰。<div id='poem_sentence_10_153377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_153377'>白衣终不至，眇眇空愁予。<div id='poem_sentence_11_153377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_153377'>今年洞庭上，九折馀崎岖。<div id='poem_sentence_12_153377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_153377'>时凭岳阳楼，山川看萦纡。<div id='poem_sentence_13_153377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_153377'>孙兄语蝉连，王丈色敷腴。<div id='poem_sentence_14_153377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_153377'>不用踏筵舞，秋风摇菊株。<div id='poem_sentence_15_153377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作何）</span>言知机早，政尔因鲈鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_21_153377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_153377'>分襟肺肝<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作肝肺）</span>热，抚事岁月迂。<div id='poem_sentence_22_153377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_153377'>归家问瓶锡，生理何必馀。<div id='poem_sentence_25_153377'>回首望尧云，中原莽榛芜。<div id='poem_sentence_25_153377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_153377'>臣岂专爱死，有怀竟不舒。<div id='poem_sentence_26_153377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_153377'>老谋与壮事，二者惭俱无。<div id='poem_sentence_27_153377_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 原作几，据须溪本、四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_153377_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年9月</a>　有诗送王接之子赴试。作品：《送王因叔赴试》<div id='poem_153295' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153295' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/153295?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送王因叔赴试<span id='poem_content_153129'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153129'>渔子牧儿谈笑新，先生胜日步湖漘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153129'>沙边忽见长身士，头上仍攲折角巾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153129'>豺虎不能宽远俗，山川终要识诗人。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153129'>芦丛如画斜阳里，拄杖相寻无杂宾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153129_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_153134")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_153134_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153134'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153134'>洞庭微雨后，凉气入纶巾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153134_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153134'>水底归云乱，芦丛返照新。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153134_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153134'>遥汀横薄暮，独鸟度长津。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153134_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153134'>兵甲无归日，江湖送老身。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153134_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153134'>悠悠只倚杖，悄悄自伤神。<div id='poem_sentence_4_153134_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_153134'>天意苍茫里，村醪亦醉人。<div id='poem_sentence_5_153134_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_153134'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_153134_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
华容
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b84dd73497d64379a80effd5b0ac5a8c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b84dd73497d64379a80effd5b0ac5a8c");'><span id='b84dd73497d64379a80effd5b0ac5a8c_link' href='/Writing/153236?labeling=true' target='_blank'>舟抵华容县</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_153236'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153236'>篙舟入华容，白水绕<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>城堞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153236'>夹津列茂树，倒影青相接。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153236'>远色分村坞，微凉动芦叶。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153236'>天地困腐儒，江湖托孤楫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153236'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_153236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_153236'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_153236_0'>⑴ 原作满，据须溪本、四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_153236_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_153178' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153178' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/153178?labeling=true' target='_blank'>月夜</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_153178'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153178'>独立夜轇轕，芦声泛遥津。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153178'>月下风起波，莽莽白龙鳞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153178'>阴彩凝草木，暑气森星辰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153178'>天地尘未消，江湖气聊伸。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153178'>人生几今夕，乱代偶此身。<div id='poem_sentence_4_153178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_153178'>胡为不少乐，况乃迹易陈。<div id='poem_sentence_5_153178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_153178'>三更大鱼舞，悄怆惊心神。<div id='poem_sentence_6_153178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_153178'>永怀骑鲸士，发兴烟中新。<div id='poem_sentence_7_153178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_153178'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_153178_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_153333' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153333' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/153333?labeling=true' "poem_title_153333")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_153333_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153333'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153333'>幽卧不知晴，樯梢见斜日。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153333'>披衣起四望，天际山争出。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153333'>光辉渚蒲净，意气沙鸥逸。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_153333'>腐儒徒叹嗟<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作嗟叹）</span>，救弊知无术。<div id='poem_sentence_7_153333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_153333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_153333'>念此百年内，可复受忧戚。<div id='poem_sentence_10_153333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_153333'>林木<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>方翳然，放怀陶兹夕。<div id='poem_sentence_11_153333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_153333'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_153333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_153333'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_6_153333_0'>⑴ 原作伐，据须溪本、四库本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_11_153333_0'>⑵ 原作水，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_153333_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_153121' class='_poem'><div -----title
湘潭
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ab5b05a60385492398945fbecf5b7326_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ab5b05a60385492398945fbecf5b7326");'><span id='ab5b05a60385492398945fbecf5b7326_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　由南洋路去湘潭，道中有诗。作品：《奇父先至湘阴书来戒由禄唐路而仆以它故由南阳路来夹道皆松如行青罗步障中先寄奇父》<span class='inlineComment2'>（该诗作于去湘潭道中，姑系于湘潭。）</span>《初识茶花》<span class='inlineComment2'>（该诗作于去湘潭道中，姑系于湘潭。）</span><div id='poem_153262' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153262' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/153262?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奇父先至湘阴书来戒由禄唐路而仆以它故由南阳<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>路来夹道皆松如行青罗步障中先寄奇父</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_153262")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_153262_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_153262_0'>① 原作洋，据四库本改</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153262'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153262'>云接湘阴百里松，肃肃穆穆湖南风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153262'>随时忧乐非人世<span class='inlineComment2'>（须溪本、四库本作事）</span>，迎我笙箫起道中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153262'>竹舆两面天明灭，秋令不到林西东。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153262_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153262'>未必禄唐能办此，题诗著画寄兴公。<div id='poem_sentence_0_152837'>伊轧篮舆不受催，湖南秋色更佳哉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_152837_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_152837'>青裙玉面初相识，九月<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_2_152837'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_152837_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年11月</a>　抵潭州。仲冬，以玉刚卯为其帅向子諲寿，有诗。作品：《以玉刚卯为向伯共生朝》<div id='poem_153393' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153393' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/153393?labeling=true' target='_blank'>以玉刚卯为向伯共生朝<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_content_153393'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153393'>仲冬吉日，风穆气休。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153393_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153393'>我出刚卯，以寿元侯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153393_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153393'>祝融之玉，莫此<span id='poem_note_153393_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　旋去潭，有诗。作品：《别伯恭》《再别》《别孙信道》<div id='poem_152980' id='poem_sentence_0_152980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_152980'>公为九州督，我是半途人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_152980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153020_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153020'>极知身有几，不奈世相违。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153020_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----end



-----title
长沙
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f1450cc062544e35a693503254ec9242_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f1450cc062544e35a693503254ec9242");'><span id='f1450cc062544e35a693503254ec9242_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　秋，自紫阳入邵州，出石限，小病，有诗。作品：《石限病起》<div id='poem_152808' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_152808' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_152808'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_152808'>幽人病起山深处，小院鸦鸣日午时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_152808_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153374'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153374'>忆昨炎正中不融，元帅仗钺临山东。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153374'>万方嗷嗷叫上帝，黄屋已照睢阳宫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153374'>呜呼吾君天所立，岂料四载犹服戎。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153374'>禹巡会稽不到海，未省驾舶观民风。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153374'>定知谏诤有张猛，不可危急无高共。<div id='poem_sentence_4_153374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_153374'>自古美恶周必复，犬羊汝莫穷妖凶。<div id='poem_sentence_5_153374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_153374'>吉语四奏元气通<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作道，据须溪本、四库本改）</span>，德音夜发春改容。<div id='poem_sentence_6_153374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_153374'>雷雨一日遍天下，父老感泣沾其胸。<div id='poem_sentence_7_153374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_153374'>臣少忧国今成翁，欲起荷戟伤疲癃。<div id='poem_sentence_8_153374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_153374'>小游太一未移次，大树将军莫振功。<div id='poem_sentence_9_153374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_153374'>刘琨祖逖未足雄，晏球一战腥臊空。<div id='poem_sentence_10_153374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_153374'>诸君努力光竹素，天子可使尘常蒙。<div id='poem_sentence_11_153374_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_153374'>君不见夷门山头虎复龙，向来佳气元葱葱。<div 永州

道县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='9c447fe3254048f6b45a58c2a3b0bd5c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9c447fe3254048f6b45a58c2a3b0bd5c");'><span id='9c447fe3254048f6b45a58c2a3b0bd5c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>，41岁</div><div id='9c447fe3254048f6b45a58c2a3b0bd5c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年11月20日</a>　十一月二十日过道州，为姜仲谦题任才仲画轴。作品：《明年十一月二十日南游过道州谒姜光彦出才仲画轴则写是夕事也剪烛观之恍然一笑书八句以当画记》<div id='poem_153159' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153159' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/153159?labeling=true' target='_blank'>己酉中秋之夕与任才仲醉于岳阳楼上明年十一月二十日南游过道<span class='inlineComment2'>（须溪本下有州字）</span>谒姜光彦出才仲画轴则写是夕事也剪烛观之恍然一笑书八句以当画记<span class='inlineComment2'>（原注：光彦名仲谦，尝任湖北漕。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年11月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_153159")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_153159_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153159'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153159'>去年中秋洞庭野，寒瑶万顷兼天泻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153159'>岳阳楼上两幅巾，月入栏干影潇洒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153159'>世间此影<span class='inlineComment2'>（须溪本作境）</span>谁能孤，狂如我友人所无。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153159'>一梦经年无续处，道州还见倚楼图。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153159'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_153159_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

id='poem_sentence_7_153361_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_153361'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_153361_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_153361_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_153059' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153059' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/153059?labeling=true' 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>度庾岭，上罗浮。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
绍兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c7e4bee8c15848778ae0b4e5eeee08d7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c7e4bee8c15848778ae0b4e5eeee08d7");'><span id='c7e4bee8c15848778ae0b4e5eeee08d7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>，42岁</div><div id='c7e4bee8c15848778ae0b4e5eeee08d7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　夏，抵会稽行在所，继除兵部员外郎，有诗。作品：《送熊博士赴瑞安令》<div id='poem_153076' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153076' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/153076?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送熊博士赴瑞安令<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_153076")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_153076_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_153076_0'>① 原注：熊名彦诗，字叔雅，番阳人，尝为祠部郎、知永州。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153076'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153076'>衣冠衮衮相逢地<span class='inlineComment2'>（须溪本、四库本作处）</span>，草木萧萧未变时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153076_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153076'>聚散同惊一枕梦，悲欢各诵十年诗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153076_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153076'>山林有约吾当去<span class='inlineComment2'>（须溪本增注：闽本作老。）</span>，天地无情子亦饥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153076_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153076'>笑领铜章非失计，岁寒心事欲深期。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153076_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153076'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_153076_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年8月</a>　秋八月，迁起居郎，有诗。作品：《喜雨》《醉中》<div id='poem_153342' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153342' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_153342")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_153342_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153342'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153342'>秦望山头云，昨日鸾凤举。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153342'>冥冥万里风<span class='inlineComment2'>（须溪本作润）</span>，淅淅三更雨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153342'>小臣知君忧，起坐听檐语。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153342'>风力有去来，龙工杂文武。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153342'>灯花识我意，一笑相媚妩。<div id='poem_sentence_4_153342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_153342'>泥翻早朝路，㳽㳽光欲吐。<div id='poem_sentence_5_153342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_153342'>郁然苍龙阙，佳气接南亩。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年7月</a>　是秋，所作词颇多。立秋后三日，作《虞美人》（扁舟三日秋塘语）<div id='poem_153413' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_153413' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_153413")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_153413_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_153413'>余甲寅岁，自春官出守湖州。秋杪道 中，荷花无复存者。乙卯岁，自琐闼以病得请奉祠。卜居青墩。立秋后三日行，舟之前后，如朝霞相映，望之不断也。以长短句记之</div><div id='poem_preface_153413_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_153413'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_153413'>扁舟三日秋塘路。平度荷花去。<div id='poem_sentence_0_153413_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_153413'>病夫因病得来游。更值满川微雨、洗新秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_153413_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_153413'>去年长恨拿舟晚。空见残荷满。<div id='poem_sentence_2_153413_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_153413'>今年何以报君恩。一路繁花相送、过青墩。<div id='poem_sentence_3_153413_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_153413'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_153413_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_153413'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(153413)'>评注</a><span id='poem_sentence_0_152865'>黯黯当窗云不驱，不教风日到琴书。<div id='poem_sentence_0_152865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_152865'>只今老子风流地，何似茅山陶隐居。<div id='poem_sentence_1_152865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_152865'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_152865_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
衢州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='cc911df6c50f407294d721627a69edbf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cc911df6c50f407294d721627a69edbf");'><span id='cc911df6c50f407294d721627a69edbf_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年</a>，46岁</div><div id='cc911df6c50f407294d721627a69edbf' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年</a>　是秋，尝一至衢州，与赵子昼、程俱唱酬。作品：《题崇兰图》<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
苏州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2ce8c2d86e554ef997b5c995bde50566_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2ce8c2d86e554ef997b5c995bde50566");'><span id='2ce8c2d86e554ef997b5c995bde50566_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1137')">1136-1137年</a>，47-48岁</div><div id='2ce8c2d86e554ef997b5c995bde50566' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年9月</a>　秋九月，从帝幸平江。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年11月</a>　冬十一月辛未，除翰林学士知制诰。作品：《玉堂儤直》<div id='poem_152806' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_152806' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/152806?labeling=true' target='_blank'>玉堂儤直</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34486, "宋", "陈与义", "poem_title_152806")'>陈与义</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_152806_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_152806'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_152806'>庭叶珑珑晓更青，断云吐日照寒厅。<div id='poem_sentence_0_152806_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_152806'>只应未上归田奏，贪诵楞伽四卷经。<div id='poem_sentence_1_152806_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_152806'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_152806_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　尝奉召定《法帖》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年1月</a>　春正月癸未，除左中大夫参知政事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年2月</a>　二月甲辰，奉诏撰徽宗谥册文。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南京
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ae57b290dea14d2185a8ea7b47e72844_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ae57b290dea14d2185a8ea7b47e72844");'><span id='ae57b290dea14d2185a8ea7b47e72844_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1138')">1137-1138年</a>，48-49岁</div><div id='ae57b290dea14d2185a8ea7b47e72844' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年3月</a>　三月，从幸建康。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年3月</a>　三月壬申，命分治户、刑、工房。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年6月</a>　六月己酉，奉诏撰显恭皇后谥册文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年7月</a>　七月丁卯，因张戒外任，言养成人才。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年8月</a>　八月戊戌，郦琼叛。壬寅，论淮西形式。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年9月</a>　九月丁卯，张俊移屯庐州，为请赐僦舟钱万缗，不允。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年10月</a>　冬十月癸卯，与赵鼎、张守等论“虔贼”事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年1月</a>　春正月癸巳，尝论堂陛之势。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年1月</a>　是月乙巳，论用兵。<br /></div>
-----end
